Gonna be the pedantic cunt to point out that Vicious Mockery doesn't have an attack roll, but rather the target gets a Wisdom saving throw, so no nat 20 or chance to crit. Also only does 1d4 but can go up to 4d4 at level 17. So my head canon here is that your bard is a full level 20 near-godlike adventurer and just unleashed hell on this child. As you should; probably the kind of kid to lose a ring at a wedding.
